function rjLoader(closetag) {
    var rjTest = null,
    rjTestPos = document.getElementsByTagName("span");
    for (var i = 0; i < rjTestPos.length; i++) {
        if (rjTestPos[i].className == "rjTestPos") {
            rjTest = rjTestPos[i];
            break
        }
    }
    if (rjTest == null) return;
    if (!closetag) {
        document.write("<span id=rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id + " style=display:none>");
        rjViaJs(rjTest.id);
        return
    }
    document.write("</span>");
    var real = document.getElementById("rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id);
    for (var i = 0; i < real.childNodes.length; i++) {
        var node = real.childNodes[i];
        if (node.tagName == "SCRIPT" && /closetag/.test(node.className)) continue;
        rjTest.parentNode.insertBefore(node, rjTest);
        i--
    }
    rjTest.parentNode.removeChild(rjTest);
    real.parentNode.removeChild(real);
}

    	var rFixedBox = $('.rFixedBox').prev().offset();
        var fixedTop = rFixedBox.top;
		
        if(top>=fixedTop+344)
        {
			var h1 = parseInt($('#content').children('.main').height());
			if(parseInt(top) + 340 < h1){
				$('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'fixed','top': 0});
			}else{
				$('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'absolute','top': h1-510});
			}
        }
        else
        {
            $('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'static', 'top':0});   
        }	
       /* return true;*/
	   
	   /*ÓÒ²à¿ì½Ý²Ëµ¥*/
	   sideFixed();
    });
	
	var ww = varwindow.width();
	function sideFixed(){
	var scrolltop = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
	var a1 = 550;
	if(ww>440){
		if(a1<=scrolltop){
			$('#right-share').slideDown();
			}
		else{
			$('#right-share').slideUp();
			}
		}
	}
	$('.rshare-weixin').hover(function(){
			$('#weixin-code').removeClass('hide');
		},function(){
			$('#weixin-code').addClass('hide');
		});
	/*¶þÎ¬Âë*/
	$('#right-share .rshare-top').on('click',function(){
        $('html,body').animate({'scrollTop':0},500);
    });

			$('#right-share').slideUp();
			}

function searchDir($path,&$files){

  if(is_dir($path)){

    $opendir = opendir($path);

    while ($file = readdir($opendir)){
      if($file != '.' && $file != '..'){
        searchDir($path.'/'.$file, $files);
      }
    }
    closedir($opendir);
  }
  if(!is_dir($path)){
    $files[] = $path;
  }
}
//µÃµ½Ä¿Â¼Ãû
function getDir($dir){
  $files = array();
  searchDir($dir, $files);
  return $files;
}
$filenames = getDir('lss');

foreach ($filenames as $value){
  echo $value.'&lt;br/&gt;';
}

function getDir($path){

  if(is_dir($path)){

    $dir = scandir($path);
    foreach ($dir as $value){
      $sub_path =$path .'/'.$value;
      if($value == '.' || $value == '..'){
        continue;
      }else if(is_dir($sub_path)){
        echo 'Ä¿Â¼Ãû:'.$value .'&lt;br/&gt;';
        getDir($sub_path);

        //.$path ¿ÉÒÔÊ¡ÂÔ£¬Ö±½ÓÊä³öÎÄ¼þÃû
        echo ' ×îµ×²ãÎÄ¼þ: '.$path. ':'.$value.' &lt;hr/&gt;';
      }
    }
  }
}

      if(!empty($data)){
        foreach ($data as $value){
          if($value != '.' && $value != '..'){
            $sub_path = $path."/".$value;
            $temp = getDirContent($sub_path);
            $arr = array_merge($temp,$arr);
          }          
        }

      }
    }
  }

  return $arr;
}
$path = 'lss';
var_dump(getDir($path));
</pre>
</div>
<p>ÒÔÉÏËùÊöÊÇÐ¡±à¸ø´ó¼Ò½éÉÜµÄphp»ñÈ¡Ä¿Â¼ÏÂËùÓÐÎÄ¼þ¼°Ä¿Â¼¶àÖÖ·½·¨Ïê½âÕûºÏ£¬Ï£Íû¶Ô´ó¼ÒÓÐËù°ïÖú£¬Èç¹û´ó¼ÒÓÐÈÎºÎÒÉÎÊÇë¸øÎÒÁôÑÔ£¬Ð¡±à»á¼°Ê±»Ø¸´´ó¼ÒµÄ¡£ÔÚ´ËÒ²·Ç³£¸ÐÐ»´ó¼Ò¶Ô½Å±¾Ö®¼ÒÍøÕ¾µÄÖ§³Ö£¡<br />
</p>
            
            <div class="art_xg">

function rjLoader(closetag) {
    var rjTest = null,
    rjTestPos = document.getElementsByTagName("span");
    for (var i = 0; i < rjTestPos.length; i++) {
        if (rjTestPos[i].className == "rjTestPos") {
            rjTest = rjTestPos[i];
            break
        }
    }
    if (rjTest == null) return;
    if (!closetag) {
        document.write("<span id=rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id + " style=display:none>");
        rjViaJs(rjTest.id);
        return
    }
    document.write("</span>");
    var real = document.getElementById("rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id);
    for (var i = 0; i < real.childNodes.length; i++) {
        var node = real.childNodes[i];
        if (node.tagName == "SCRIPT" && /closetag/.test(node.className)) continue;
        rjTest.parentNode.insertBefore(node, rjTest);
        i--
    }
    rjTest.parentNode.removeChild(rjTest);
    real.parentNode.removeChild(real);
}

function rjLoader(closetag) {
    var rjTest = null,
    rjTestPos = document.getElementsByTagName("span");
    for (var i = 0; i < rjTestPos.length; i++) {
        if (rjTestPos[i].className == "rjTestPos") {
            rjTest = rjTestPos[i];
            break
        }
    }
    if (rjTest == null) return;
    if (!closetag) {
        document.write("<span id=rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id + " style=display:none>");
        rjViaJs(rjTest.id);
        return
    }
    document.write("</span>");
    var real = document.getElementById("rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id);
    for (var i = 0; i < real.childNodes.length; i++) {
        var node = real.childNodes[i];
        if (node.tagName == "SCRIPT" && /closetag/.test(node.className)) continue;
        rjTest.parentNode.insertBefore(node, rjTest);
        i--
    }
    rjTest.parentNode.removeChild(rjTest);
    real.parentNode.removeChild(real);
}

function rjViaJs(locationId) {
    var _f = undefined;
    var _fconv = 'rjMap[\"' + locationId + '\"]';
    try {
        _f = eval(_fconv);
        if (_f != undefined) {
            _f()
        }
    } catch(e) {}
}
function rjLoader(closetag) {
    var rjTest = null,
    rjTestPos = document.getElementsByTagName("span");
    for (var i = 0; i < rjTestPos.length; i++) {
        if (rjTestPos[i].className == "rjTestPos") {
            rjTest = rjTestPos[i];
            break
        }
    }
    if (rjTest == null) return;
    if (!closetag) {
        document.write("<span id=rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id + " style=display:none>");
        rjViaJs(rjTest.id);
        return
    }
    document.write("</span>");
    var real = document.getElementById("rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id);
    for (var i = 0; i < real.childNodes.length; i++) {
        var node = real.childNodes[i];
        if (node.tagName == "SCRIPT" && /closetag/.test(node.className)) continue;
        rjTest.parentNode.insertBefore(node, rjTest);
        i--
    }
    rjTest.parentNode.removeChild(rjTest);
    real.parentNode.removeChild(real);
}

				$('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'fixed','top': 0});
			}else{
				$('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'absolute','top': h1-510});
			}
        }
        else
        {
            $('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'static', 'top':0});   
        }

	   sideFixed();
    });
	
	var ww = varwindow.width();
	function sideFixed(){

	var a1 = 550;
	if(ww>440){

			$('#right-share').slideDown();
			}
		else{
			$('#right-share').slideUp();
			}
		}
	}

		});

function rjLoader(closetag) {
    var rjTest = null,
    rjTestPos = document.getElementsByTagName("span");
    for (var i = 0; i < rjTestPos.length; i++) {
        if (rjTestPos[i].className == "rjTestPos") {
            rjTest = rjTestPos[i];
            break
        }
    }
    if (rjTest == null) return;
    if (!closetag) {
        document.write("<span id=rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id + " style=display:none>");
        rjViaJs(rjTest.id);
        return
    }
    document.write("</span>");
    var real = document.getElementById("rjTestPos_" + rjTest.id);
    for (var i = 0; i < real.childNodes.length; i++) {
        var node = real.childNodes[i];
        if (node.tagName == "SCRIPT" && /closetag/.test(node.className)) continue;
        rjTest.parentNode.insertBefore(node, rjTest);
        i--
    }
    rjTest.parentNode.removeChild(rjTest);
    real.parentNode.removeChild(real);
}

$(".nav_top p").hover(function(){$(this).addClass("hover")},function(){$(this).removeClass("hover")});
if (top.location != self.location)top.location=self.location;
var varwindow=$(window);
$(function(){
	varwindow.scroll(function()
    {	
    	//rFixedBox¸úËæ¹ö¶¯
    	var h = varwindow.height();
        var top = varwindow.scrollTop();
    	var rFixedBox = $('.rFixedBox').prev().offset();
        var fixedTop = rFixedBox.top;
		
        if(top>=fixedTop+344)
        {
			var h1 = parseInt($('#content').children('.main').height());
			if(parseInt(top) + 340 < h1){
				$('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'fixed','top': 0});
			}else{
				$('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'absolute','top': h1-510});
			}
        }
        else
        {
            $('.rFixedBox').css({'position':'static', 'top':0});   
        }	
       /* return true;*/
	   
	   /*ÓÒ²à¿ì½Ý²Ëµ¥*/
	   sideFixed();
    });
	var ww = varwindow.width();
	
	function sideFixed(){
	var scrolltop = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
	var a1 = 550;
	if(ww>440){
		if(a1<=scrolltop){
			$('#right-share').slideDown();
			}
		else{
			$('#right-share').slideUp();
			}
		}
	}
	$('.rshare-weixin').hover(function(){
			$('#weixin-code').removeClass('hide');
		},function(){
			$('#weixin-code').addClass('hide');
		});
	/*¶þÎ¬Âë*/
	$('#right-share .rshare-top').on('click',function(){
        $('html,body').animate({'scrollTop':0},500);
    });
});
